Event</a></h1>\n\n\t\t\t<abbr class=\"entry-date published updated\" title=\"2017-04-23T12:00:53+00:00\">April 23, 2017</abbr>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t<a tag\">2017 Fantasy Baseball Buy/Sell</a>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"comments-link\"><a href=\"http://razzball.com/mitch-a-palooza-seattles-sultry-new-event/#comments\">62&nbsp;Comments</a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"by vcard\">by: <span><a href=\"http://razzball.com/author/tehol-beddict/\" rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">Tehol Beddict</a></span></p>\n\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p>Wait, what? The Mariners got Jean Segura AND <strong><a href=\"/player/Mitch+Haniger/\" target=\"_blank\">Mitch Haniger</a></strong> for the continually underachieving Tai Walker? The same Haniger who’s third in offensive WAR in the AL (through Friday), first in the AL in runs scored with 16, leading the AL in times on base, fourth in the clubhouse in jersey-chaser takedowns, and first in my heart for being part of the heist that was the Taijuan Walker trade. Coming off a year where he masta-donged 25 and 94 with a .321 BA in AA/AAA last year, the D-Bags felt the urge to dump another diamond in the rough, a la Max Scherzer. I’m still trying to wrap my head around that trade all those year ago. I couldn’t believe at the time and couldn’t believe they weren’t making a bigger deal about it.</p>\n<p>I may be going too far as I’m a Walker fan, but Haniger clearly has All-star capabilities and hitting in this loaded lineup is going to keep him relevant all season long. Much unlike myself, it’s really easy to be a fan of this dude.</p>\n<p>Here’s what else intrigued me this past week… Take heed!</p>\n<a href=\"http://razzball.com/mitch-a-palooza-seattles-sultry-new-event/\" class=\"read_more\">Please, blog, may I have some more?</a>\t</div><!-- .entry-summary -->\n</article><!-- #post-1451360 status-publish format-standard hentry category-2017-fantasy-baseball category-this-week-in-razzball tag-anthony-senzatela tag-brandon-mccarthy tag-chase-headley tag-chris-sale tag-clayton-kershaw tag-cole-hamels tag-eric-thames tag-gerrit-cole tag-hyun-jin-ryu tag-jason-vargas tag-joey-gallo tag-madison-bumgarner tag-michael-wacha tag-sal-romano tag-starling-marte tag-zack-grienke pmpro-has-access\">\n\t<header class=\"entry-header\">\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t<img src=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/uploads/userphoto/500.jpg\" alt=\"Viz\" width=\"100\" height=\"100\" class=\"photo\">\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title\"><a href=\"http://razzball.com/week-razz-week-3/\" title=\"Permalink to This Week in Razz, Week 3\" rel=\"bookmark\">This Week in Razz, Week 3</a></h1>\n\n\t\t\t<abbr class=\"entry-date published updated\" title=\"2017-04-23T11:00:15+00:00\">April 23, 2017</abbr>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t<a href=\"http://razzball.com/category/2017-fantasy-baseball/\" rel=\"category tag\">2017 Fantasy Baseball</a>, <a href=\"http://razzball.com/category/this-week-in-razzball/\" rel=\"category tag\">This Week in Razzball</a>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"comments-link\"><a href=\"http://razzball.com/week-razz-week-3/#comments\">2&nbsp;Comments</a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"by vcard\">by: <span><a href=\"http://razzball.com/author/viza/\" rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">Viz</a></span></p>\n\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p>Moving the standard disabled list to 10 days from 15 was a horrific decision by Major League Baseball.  If a pitcher is going to miss one start, a team can just throw him on the DL now and get that extra body up in his place.  I wouldn’t be surprised if half of the starting pitchers in the majors end up on the disabled list for that reason.  In the past, when a batter was going to be out for a week, teams had to make a decision whether to force him out another week by putting him on the DL or waiting it out.  Now, teams are going to defer to putting the player on the DL.  That’s where the biggest fantasy impact is going to come.  We’ve already seen a bunch of players go on the 10-day DL and come off immediately when the 10 days are up.  On most of my teams, I’ve had 3-6 players on the DL at the same time already and we’re only three weeks into the season.  I think the use of the disabled list is going to increase by a fairly wide margin so I suggest that your league has at least 3 DL spots going forward.  The more players that go on the list, the more spots you should have.  Anyways, let’s take a look at what was posted on Razzball this week, including a bunch of different articles that can help you with injuries:</p>\n<a href=\"http://razzball.com/week-razz-week-3/\" class=\"read_more\">Please, blog, may I have some more?</a>\t</div><!-- .entry-summary -->\n</article><!-- #post-1451947 -->\n\n &nbsp; <a href=\"http://razzball.com/pigeons-table-grey-albright/\" target=\"_blank\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1408342 size-full\" src=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/pigeons-on-a-table-ad-460x60.gif\" width=\"460\" height=\"60\"></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\n\n<article id=\"post-1450271\" class=\"post-1450271 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-2017-fantasy-baseball category-2017-ops-leagues tag-aaron-hicks tag-avisail-garcia tag-chase-headley tag-eric-thames tag-fantasy-baseball-ops tag-fantasy-baseball-ops-leagues tag-josh-bell tag-ryon-healy tag-trey-mancini tag-zack-cozart pmpro-has-access\">\n\t<header class=\"entry-header\">\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t<img src=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/uploads/userphoto/532.png\" alt=\"Phil B.\" width=\"100\" height=\"99\" class=\"photo\">\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title\"><a href=\"http://razzball.com/ops-leaguers-unite-thanks-for-the-tickets/\" title=\"Permalink to OPS Leaguers Unite! &nbsp;DFS on the regular isn’t easy, but add in the uncertainty of playing time, crazy weather, early slumps, offseason adjustments, new teams, new teammates and there are a lot of extra factors. &nbsp;It’s for this reason I tend to ease myself into the DFS waters. &nbsp;I take it pretty slow in April while we let some data collect. &nbsp;When May hits we can start ramping it up and really be ripping come June. &nbsp;We’ve got three weeks worth of data to work with so far and&nbsp;<strong>Ivan Nova&nbsp;</strong>($15,600) has been fantastic. &nbsp;The strikeouts have been a bit lacking but it’s hard to quibble with a 2.25 ERA and a sub 1.00 WHIP. &nbsp;If you are prone to quibbling, I’d point out that Nova is smack dab in the middle of the road for pricing today, allowing you to afford those sweet Coors bats we all crave. &nbsp;Plus, I mean, come on, #RevengeGame, #EnoughSaid.</p>\n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">New to </span></i><a class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p>With roughly two months worth of baseball activity behind us, it’s time to re-rank some stuff. Sure, that’s an awful reason to rank things, and what’s baseball activity anyway? But Keith Law gets to update his after a couple of months, so why can’t cha boy Ralphie L? Some things have changed, for sure, some top prospects have either graduated, or are on the cusp of graduating. Most notably Andrew Benintendi, Dansby Swanson, Hunter Renfroe, Manuel Margot, Aaron Judge, and Tyler Glasnow. I figure if you’re in the majors, I ain’t gonna rank ya no more. There’s been a few jumps, the most significant of which is Chicago Cubs prospect Ian Happ. For those of you who don’t follow minor league box scores, he’s pretty much the Eric Thames of the minors leagues. Only minus the beard or the Popeye muscles. My excitement over Lewis Brinson and Cody Bellinger should be easily identified, they slot second and third respectively. As for the rest of the list you’re going to have to see for yourself. No, I won’t be sliding Tyler Mahle into my Top 25, after the perfect game last night. </span>\n\t\t\t<a href=\"http://razzball.com/category/2017-fantasy-baseball/\" rel=\"category tag\">2017 Fantasy Baseball</a>, <a href=\"http://razzball.com/category/two-start-fantasy-starters/\" href=\"http://razzball.com/two-start-starters-week-4-wait-jason-vargas/#comments\">13&nbsp;Comments</a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"by vcard\">by: <span><a href=\"http://razzball.com/author/matthayes/\" rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">M@</a></span></p>\n\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/vargasoooo.gif\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1450649\" src=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/vargasoooo.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"542\" height=\"300\"></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">In a week where Clayton Kershaw is slated for two starts (pour one out for that first one. It should have been another epic matchup of Madison Bumgarner against King Kershaw, but alas…<a href=\"https://gfycat.com/VibrantCourteousDeermouse\">dirt bikes</a>. Ugh!), the pitcher drawing the most attention, or at least the most reaction like the one above, is from none of other than the guy doing the reaction above! It’s like those Gronk wearing a shirt of Edelman, wearing a shirt of Gronk, wearing a shirt of Edelman things. You’ll get through this. I promise. And no more mention of anything Boston in this post. You have my word. (Still butt hurt about the Super Bowl. Always will be.)</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">Now, back to the matters at hand. Jason Vargas. Jason freaking Vargas. I was in an AL-Only auction at the end of March. $270 budget, 33 roster spots, 10 teams. Jason Vargas? Thrown out around #300 and went for a cool $2. I mean, who in the I want to cuss right now ever saw this coming? Certainly not ol’ Vargas himself. Why? Because this version of Vargas, the 34 year-old version, is every bit the same version as last 11 years who never held a K/9 north of 7 when pitching more than 12 IP in a year. And yet, here we are in Week 4 and Vargas is the ever-deserving candidate to be highlighted leading into this week, joining the echelon previously only befitted by Kershaw and MadBum.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><a href=\"http://www.fangraphs.com/fantasy/tipping-pitches-jason-vargas-is-dominating/\">Paul Sporer at FanGraphs</a> said, “Jason Vargas is pitching out of his mind right now…His velocity has always been underwhelming (~86-88 mph) and it’s on the low end this year at 86.6. Vargas is using essentially the same pitch mix, too…I don’t really know what to make of this.” It’s a fascinating article that shines some light on the deeper stats of Jason’s breakout. Go nerd out for a bit after you finish here, because somewhere between his last healthy season in 2014 and now a beast has emerged. An 87 MPH beast. Can it last? Let’s hope it continues for at least his next two!</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">(For the record, I nailed the Eric Thames Top 100 and Andrew Triggs <a href=\"http://razzball.com/two-starts-starters-week-3-oakland-wins-with-triggs-onometry/\">Two-Starts</a> highlights last week. That probably means Vargas implodes this week, haha.)</p>\n<p><em>Pitchers are listed in order by rank.&nbsp;Colors represent <strong><span style=\"color: #ff0000;\">8 toughest</span></strong>&nbsp;or rel=\"bookmark\">Biking Bumgarner Bail Out a Big Bummer</a></h1>\n\n\t\t\t<abbr class=\"entry-date published updated\" title=\"2017-04-22T09:05:11+00:00\">April 22, 2017</abbr>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t<a href=\"http://razzball.com/category/2017-fantasy-baseball/\" rel=\"category tag\">2017 Fantasy Baseball</a>, <a href=\"http://razzball.com/category/fantasy-baseball-daily-notes/\" rel=\"category tag\">Fantasy Baseball Daily Notes</a>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"comments-link\"><a href=\"http://razzball.com/biking-bumgarner-bail-out-a-big-bummer/#comments\">81&nbsp;Comments</a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"by vcard\">by: <span><a href=\"http://razzball.com/author/blairtch/\" rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">Dan Pants</a></span></p>\n\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p>There’s no denying that <strong><a href=\"/player/Madison+Bumgarner/\" target=\"_blank\">Madison Bumgarner</a></strong> works hard. Well, he plays even harder. So it should have come as no surprise when news broke that the San Francisco ace was placed on the disabled list after injuring his left shoulder in a dirt bike accident. Wait. You were doing WHAT? But why!? You can’t expect Madison to get his kicks doing regular pleb things like playing Xbox or frisbee golf, it’s gotta be EXTREME. Regardless, this is a huge blow for Giants fans and Bumgarner owners alike. Madison is sporting a 3.00 ERA, 1.07 WHIP and 28/4 K/BB rate through four starts and early reports suggest he is set to miss over two months. Bummer. But honestly, what do you want from the guy? For him to not participate in dangerous extreme sports on his days off? I mean, come on, his hands were tied. <strong><a href=\"/player/Ty+Blach/\" target=\"_blank\">Ty Blach</a></strong> is set to fill in the interim. Blach and his just 21.2 innings of major league experience. Blach is a ground ball pitcher with just a 13.4% strikeout rate, so he’s probably not the answer to your Bumgarner woes. More like, Ty Blech, right? Lol. He is slated to take on the Dodgers next week, but if you’re feeling dangerous you’d likely be better off dirt biking than&nbsp;picking up Ty Blach outside of deep NL-Only leagues. Here’s hoping at the very least Bumgarner got some sick air.</p>\n<p>Here’s what else I saw in fantasy baseball Friday night:</p>\n<a href=\"http://razzball.com/biking-bumgarner-bail-out-a-big-bummer/\" class=\"read_more\">Please, blog, may I have some more?</a>\t</div><!-- .entry-summary -->\n</article><!-- #post-1450550 -->\n\n href=\"http://razzball.com/fanduel-carlos-whispers/#respond\">Leave&nbsp;a&nbsp;comment</a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"by vcard\">by: <span><a href=\"http://razzball.com/author/vickyb/\" rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">VictoriaB</a></span></p>\n\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p>I’m with <a href=\"http://razzball.com/streamers/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Streamonator</a>: <strong>Carlos Carrasco</strong> is your No-Brainer O’ the Day. (Not to be confused with your Darren O’ the Day, which is a fish submarine sandwich.) The last time Carrasco faced the White Sox, at home, it was to the tune of 1 ER over 7 innings, and this matchup is in the more pitcher-friendly Sox park. (Mind you, his last start versus the Tigers was a tad more worrying — still only 2 ER, but he struggled with command.) But today on FanDuel, he’s $10,300. And at the same time, the Giants are in Coors. I’ve set myself a silly challenge: to play Carlos Carrasco AND stack as many Coors bats as possible, all while plugging the remaining holes as cheaply (and well? Ha) as I can. And you’ll see that through my own stubbornness, I’ve created possibly the most lopsided FanDuel lineup ever, one that will need complete rejigging if any one of my players doesn’t actually start. Like George Michael, I may come to be filled with regret and (totally logical consequence to cheating on someone!) never dance again, but it’s not for nothing that my mother calls me Victoria Mary Quite Contrary. So here goes!</p>\n<p><em>New to </em><a href=\"http://wlfanduel.adsrv.eacdn.com/C.ashx?btag=a_13485b_1419c_&amp;affid=5066&amp;siteid=13485&amp;adid=1419&amp;c=\"><em>FanDuel</em></a><em>? Headley Over Heels</a></h1>\n\n\t\t\t<abbr class=\"entry-date published updated\" title=\"2017-04-22T00:05:18+00:00\">April 22, 2017</abbr>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t<a tag\">2017 Fantasy Baseball OBP Leagues</a>\t\t\t<span class=\"sep\"> | </span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"comments-link\"><a rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">Elliot</a></span></p>\n\n\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\t<div class=\"entry-summary\">\n\t\t<p><strong><a href=\"/player/Chase+Headley/\" target=\"_blank\">Chase Headley </a>&nbsp;</strong>is a guy that I haven’t been able to get on board with, really ever. Even when he had his <strong><a href=\"/player/Brady+Anderson/\" target=\"_blank\">Brady Anderson</a></strong> year back in 2012, I couldn’t allow myself to believe that he was a top-tier ballplayer. When the Red Sox and the Yankees were both in the market for a third baseman, and <strong><a href=\"/player/Pablo+Sandoval/\" target=\"_blank\">Pablo Sandoval</a></strong> and Headley were the best bats available, the AL East superpowers each signed one. And, while the Sandoval contract has been an unmitigated disaster, Headley has actually had some middling success. He isn’t exciting, which is perhaps why I never took a liking to him. But, OBP isn’t particularly exciting either. And, it is in OBP where Headley will shine.</p>\n<a href=\"http://razzball.com/obp-leagues-headley-over-heels/\" class=\"read_more\">Please, blog, may I have some more?</a>\t</div><!-- .entry-summary rel=\"author\" class=\"url fn\">Grey</a></span></p>\n\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\n\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t<!-- Simple Share Buttons Adder (6.3.4) simplesharebuttons.com --><div class=\"ssba ssba-wrap\"><div style=\"text-align:left\"><a href=\"http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://razzball.com/2017-razzball-commenter-leagues/\" class=\"ssba_twitter_share\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/plugins/simple-share-buttons-adder/buttons/retro/twitter.png\" title=\"Twitter\" class=\"ssba ssba-img\" alt=\"Tweet about this on Twitter\"></a><a href=\"https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://razzball.com/2017-razzball-commenter-leagues/\" onclick=\"__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://razzball.com/2017-razzball-commenter-leagues/', '');\" data-site=\"\" class=\"ssba_google_share\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"http://razzball.com/wp-content/plugins/simple-share-buttons-adder/buttons/retro/google.png\" title=\"Google+\" class=\"ssba ssba-img\" alt=\"Share on Google+\"></a></div></div><p>If you’re like me on most Fridays, you’re sitting&nbsp;in your&nbsp;car beneath an underpass and writing&nbsp;ALF&nbsp;fan fiction, but today&nbsp;we have a different type of fantasy for you to&nbsp;engage in.&nbsp; No, not your fantasy where it’s you and that girl from high school in a tub of Alphabet Soup and you write her a love letter on her back in noodles! &nbsp;This is a fantasy baseball fantasy! &nbsp;Because&nbsp;you know what would be really cool? &nbsp;If you could join a<strong> fantasy baseball league</strong> that was against, like, 1000 other fantasy baseball teams. &nbsp;But not a 1000-person league, where people are trying to figure out who the back-up third baseman is on the Single-A <a href=\"http://razzball.com/teams/houston-astros\">Astros</a> affiliate, the Corpus Christi Amscrayers.&nbsp; No, this is a 12-person league designed so you compete against eleven other people in your league, then 90 other leagues of twelve.&nbsp; That would be cool.&nbsp; Oh, wait, we’ve done that. &nbsp;It’s called the Razzball Commenter Leagues, and they’re back, and you don’t even have to be a commenter to join it!&nbsp; For a limited time only, get your loved one a fantasy baseball league!&nbsp; That’s right, your hearts go pitter-patter or you’re dead on the inside (my condolences).&nbsp; Since back in June when you abandoned your fantasy baseball team because it was totally sucking and you returned to your cubbyhole of leftover Chinese food and Teddy Grahams, you’ve longed for this day.&nbsp; As Bob Marley sang, this is your redemption song, mon.&nbsp; Or womon, for our five&nbsp;girl readers.&nbsp; It’s time again to join some fantasy baseball leagues. Before you close all of your extraneous porn windows and rush to sign up, let’s explain how these fantasy baseball leagues are going to work.&nbsp; We’re going to have a bunch of leagues and crown a winner from each, then we’re going to crown ONE winner from all of the winners.&nbsp; We will be crowning the winner by taking each team’s points and multiplying it against a ‘league competitiveness factor.’&nbsp; If you want to see how it worked last year, go <a title=\"Razzball Master Standings\" href=\"http://razzball.com/standings-2016/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow\">here</a>. &nbsp;So we’re going to fill up as many fantasy leagues as we can for the next seven weeks.&nbsp; Each fantasy baseball league will be a mixed league, 12 team, snake draft, roto, 5×5, 5 OFs, one Middle Infielder, one Corner Infielder, one Utility, 9 pitchers, 20 game eligibility, 180 Games Started max, 1000 IP minimum. <strong>Like last year, we will again be going with TWO DL SLOTS</strong>. The only things you need to change from the default settings is the 180 Games Started and the TWO DL SLOTS. &nbsp;Please be vigilant about having the exact same league rules and setup as everyone else. The lineup is also known as: &nbsp;C/1B/2B/SS/3B/CI/MI/5 OF/UTIL/9 P/3 BENCH/2 DL with 180 Games Started and 1000 IP minimum.&nbsp; The fantasy leagues will be played in ESPN and they will be free to join.</p>\n<p>We’re going to start with twenty leagues of 12 and see how we do from there. To join a league… Sorry, again for the people in the back of the room:</p>\n<p><strong>TO JOIN A LEAGUE</strong><br>\nClick the LINK in the ‘League Link’ column (see below grid) and enter the PASSWORD at ESPN. Emails are there for some leagues, but you shouldn’t need to email anyone.&nbsp; You can join as many leagues as you like. &nbsp;If you join less than ten, people may make fun of you.</p>\n<p><strong>TO START A LEAGUE<br>\n</strong>Please <a href=\"http://games.espn.go.com/frontpage/baseball\" target=\"_blank\" onclick=\"__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://games.espn.go.com/frontpage/baseball', 'create a league in ESPN');\">create a league in ESPN</a> based on the league rules reference above. Step by step: Hit Create. Then Create ESPN Custom (middle option), Name League, Change to 12 Teams, Restriction Type: None, Open to All Users, Access: change to Private, create Password, leave as Roto and Snake, Make Draft Date and Time, Create. From Default settings all you have to do is change to TWO DL SLOTS and 180 Starts by pitchers. So, you go to ROSTERS and Click “Edit Roster Settings.” There, change to 2 DL Slots and 180 Starts (the counter will change to 20.0 per slot). Then SUBMIT Roster Settings. Finally, Create Your League! (Important Note: Make sure league is viewable to public but requiring a password to avoid non-Razzballers joining.) When that’s finished, <a href=\"https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/127Fr0uH0ein2ucVlldDG5eAEwwpavDbl9lEkFNN-EOI/edit?usp=sharing\" target=\"_blank\" onclick=\"__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/127Fr0uH0ein2ucVlldDG5eAEwwpavDbl9lEkFNN-EOI/edit?usp=sharing', 'click here');\">click here</a>. You will be permissioned shortly so you can add your league info to the Google Doc (the below grid cannot be edited from this page). On that Google Doc, you will need to enter your name, league link, password and please UPDATE the number of openings as your league fills up. That’s it. Oh, and don’t use your bank account password. (Here’s a <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CTVKQQbfwFY&amp;feature=youtu.be\" target=\"_blank\" onclick=\"__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=CTVKQQbfwFY&amp;feature=youtu.be', 'video');\">video</a> Jay made to help some noobs.&nbsp; Is noobs spelled with zeroes or oh’s?&nbsp; Hmm, that might make me a noob at spelling noob.)&nbsp; You can start as many leagues as you like. &nbsp;If you start less than ten leagues, again someone could mock you.</p>\n<p><strong>THE BIG PRIZE</strong></p>\n<p>You win bragging rights.&nbsp; Not just any bragging rights, but the bragging rights that you beat a thousand or so other people, and you can emphasize the “or so” as emphatically as you’d like.&nbsp; What?&nbsp; Not enough?&nbsp; Okay, for this year’s prize we’re taking the bull out of bulloney.&nbsp; We are upping the ante.&nbsp; “Hey, Olympic high jumper, can you jump over this ante?”&nbsp; No, you can’t, it’s been upped too high.&nbsp; LOOK, it’s a bird…it’s a plane…it’s our ante!&nbsp; “Excuse me, astronomer, is that a satellite orbiting earth?”&nbsp; No, son, it’s Razzball’s ante.&nbsp; They upped it.&nbsp; This year we are giving away a $250 Best Buy Gift card, which can buy just about anything (up to $250). &nbsp;I recently bought a TV that sits underneath my toilet seat so when I whizz&nbsp;I can watch TV. &nbsp;Granted, I bought this in a dream I had and I was married to Sofia Vergara in said dream, but this must exist, right? &nbsp;Also, for s’s and g’s, I’ll throw in a Razzball t-shirt because I have 14,000 of these and I’ve already outfitted all the homeless people in my neighborhood with SAGNOF t-shirts. &nbsp;But, most importantly, you will be crowned the&nbsp;2017 Razzball Commenter League Champion.&nbsp; Okay, now sign up…</p>\n<p><iframe src=\"https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/127Fr0uH0ein2ucVlldDG5eAEwwpavDbl9lEkFNN-EOI/pubhtml?widget=true&amp;headers=false\" width=\"650\" height=\"750\"></iframe></p>\t\t\n\n\n<script id=\"1hiizmo1cllyg7\" data-cfasync=\"false\">\n  (window._1hiizmo||(window._1hiizmo=[])).push({\"id\":\"1cllyg7\",\"sid\":\"1hiizmo\",\"v\":2});\n</script><div style=\"display: inline; Looking to sign up for an RCL that’s drafting when I’m awake – i.e., from 00h00 until 17h00. The period from 17h00 until 00h00 (EST) is when I sleep, more or less.</p>\n<p>b. The auditor finally finished (nice alliteration, spaz) his mission!! We can all breathe a collective sigh of relief until we discover that the situation is quite dire and we need to shape up rapidly! Oversight on monitoring the distribution of non-food items is seriously lacking! No corruption charges but we need to work on processes! The auditor told us about the distribution reports of one partner. They receive stock of 100 boxes of commodity X during the month + they have 20 boxes in stock. Then the partner distributes 90 boxes worth to our beneficiaries for the month. At month’s end, they record 20 boxes as stock for carry over into the next month instead of 30. This continues for commodities Y and Z and for months on end. Well, the only bit of good news is this all happened during the period before we arrived in the operation. The bad news is our local staff were present and just did nothing. So, there’s that.</p>\n<p>c. Have a nice weekend. A 12-team league would require 108 (12×9) pitchers to be bought.<br>\nSimilarly, for the hitters, there are 119 hitters with a non-negative dollar value. A 12-team league would require 156 (12×13) hitters to be bought.<br>\nWhy is this?<br>\nLastly, adding up all of the positive dollar values, gets $2872, when one would expect $3120
